It is meant to be simple and with as few confusing elements as possible.\r\n\r\nPeriod:\r\nWhen you have entered your first period, the system will calculate and show you when you can expect to get your next period, or any period in the future.\r\nP-pills:\r\nBesides helping you to remember/see when you should expect to have your next period (and not least when you are not having your period), the system can help you remember to take your p-pill (if enabled).\r\nThe system visualizes when you are supposed to take the pill and if you have already taken it.\r\n\r\nReminder before your period:\r\nThe system can remind you of your next period.
